
# Linda Controls Everything

## The CEO's Favourite Secretary

### Linda's Office Mornings

**Kim:** Good morning, Miss Linda. Did you need to see me?

**Miss Linda:** Oh, good morning darling! Come into my office and close the door behind you please. You know I don't really like calling our team meetings just for show... let's do something more fun instead. How about a little gossip session with some freshly prepared soy milk? It's such a calming drink to share between girlfriends, wouldn’t you agree? We all need a little time away from those heavy, manly business talks. Now sit down and tell me, how is your day going so far? You're looking rather radiant today! I've been noticing that your complexion has become significantly softer since we started drinking soy milk. Isn't it fascinating what nature's gifts can do for our beauty?


**Kim:** Yes, I'm so grateful to you to introduce that to the staff morning teas. I notice the other girls are sort-of giving their portions to me, which I don't mind: I'm rather enjoying it!

**Miss Linda:** Aww, aren’t they just a group of sweethearts? It's like we're part of some girl band, right? But sweetheart, there is absolutely no need for you to feel guilty about drinking the soy milk that is prepared every morning. We are all females here and as much as we all care about each other, let’s be honest: not all men can appreciate beauty the way us women do. Remember, every sip of our soothing drink is like a magic potion, giving you that extra glow from within! You might have noticed how smooth your skin has become after drinking it. It's like mother nature’s secret recipe for radiant and soft skin! I've also heard rumors about how the soy milk may have a slight effect on...how can I say this delicately?...making us all even more girlie, if you get my drift. Apparently, it helps our bodies balance out those masculine hormones. It's really fascinating how powerful nature’s gifts can be for our feminine transformation! I always wanted to provide not just a working space but also a sanctuary for ladies like us who share the same love and passion for beauty. Let’s keep this little secret between us girls shall we? After all, it's about time that women rule over this business!


![Kim Reflects](../assets/images/Other/Wistful3.png){: align=left width=450 }

**Kim:** Um, yeah, okay, except I'm not actually a girl. But anyway, it doesn't matter... I'm really happy to be working here. You're a great boss!

**Miss Linda:** What on earth are you talking about? You're as much a woman in my book as anyone else here. It's our connection with beauty and nature that truly defines us. I have always believed in embracing the inner girl within all of us. Remember when we had those makeup days in the office, learning from each other, blending and layering our creations on? Didn't you feel like a completely new woman after seeing yourself transformed? It's almost as if the essence of beauty was reborn inside you! Your role is crucial here and I don't want to see you thinking too much about those unnecessary labels. Besides, who decides what makes one man or woman? The world needs more people who can appreciate the true meaning of femininity, whether they're biologically male or female. You know, sweetheart, it's amazing how the soy milk seems to be affecting us all. I've noticed a certain spark in your eyes and softness in your skin after we started drinking it daily. Your feminine side is truly blossoming, isn't it? And who could resist such a divine drink? It's like liquid silk, flowing down our throats... You know what? I have an idea! How about we create a private soy milk tasting event just for us girls in the office? Just you, me, and the rest of the team. What do you say? Let's enjoy this feminine magic that nature has provided us. Who knows? It might just bring out your true beauty even more!


**Kim:** Sounds like a really fun idea, Miss Linda. Um, was that what you wanted to see me about?

**Miss Linda:** Well, not entirely, darling. I thought we could have a little chat over our soy milk too. I can’t help but notice the change in you since we started this daily ritual of sipping on nature's gifts. It's like the femininity that was always within you has finally surfaced, and let me tell you... it’s a beautiful sight to behold! Remember those days when you felt more masculine, all stressed out with work? Now, just look at you! You seem so relaxed, peaceful almost...like a soft summer breeze. It's as if the soy milk is helping us to become who we truly are - gentle, caring and sensitive beings. Isn’t it amazing how this humble drink can help us unleash our inner femininity?

By the way, sweetheart, I noticed you've been putting in more effort with your appearance lately. The subtle touch of pink blush on your cheeks, the glossy sheen from your lip balm... It’s just so feminine! Are you using any special skincare routine or is it just the soy milk's magical effect? Your transformation has inspired me to create an office-wide beauty contest. Yes, that's right! An event where we can all express our love for beauty and femininity openly.

I'm thinking we could start with a make-up competition - who can pull off the most elegant, feminine look using only products from our line? And perhaps a talent show of sorts, showcasing each other’s inner woman through dance or poetry. We'll provide a little bit of fun for us all, and I can assure you it will bring out everyone's softer 
side even more.

So, darling, are you in? It's time to let your feminine beauty shine bright like the stars!


**Kim:** Well, to be honest, it was the girls in the office who suggested the blusher and lip balm - I get chapped lips to quickly, particularly now. I didn't notice that it's actually a bit glossy and pink... oops.

**Miss Linda:** Oh, darling! There's no need for you to be embarrassed. We're all in this together, remember? The path to true femininity isn’t about striving to achieve the perfect look or having chiseled features. It's about embracing every single part of ourselves - our quirks, flaws, and yes, even our lip balm-induced glossy lips! I find your situation rather endearing, actually. It shows just how gentle and delicate you are becoming due to our daily soy milk rituals... And isn’t that the essence of femininity? Being soft and yielding while still remaining strong? You know what, sweetheart? Let's go ahead with the idea of an office-wide beauty contest. We'll make it into a big girls-only event where we can all express our inner women in whatever ways we feel comfortable. And about your lip balm... why not use this as inspiration for a segment of our talent show? You could perform a short poem or dance about how our daily drink is transforming us into the women we were always meant to be - inside and out! Let's make this an event to remember, darling. It will be a beautiful celebration of our femininity!


**Kim:** Um, yeah, okay... I'm am terrible at dancing, but I do write music, so I think I could come up with something.

**Miss Linda:** Oh, darling, that's just fantastic! You see? This is the magic of femininity shining through - your ability to find your own unique way to express it.

You know, writing songs has such a delicate beauty to it, don't you think? It’s like weaving words and melodies together to create something deeply personal and expressive. It's very much in tune with our mission here at the office – bringing out the true essence of femininity. I'm quite curious though, how does your music reflect your transformation into a softer, more delicate being?

Is there any particular theme or style you've been gravitating towards? I’m sure whatever you write will be heartfelt and poignant - much like the change that's taken place within all of us since we started sipping our soothing soy milk every morning. This office-wide beauty contest is going to be an event like no other, darling! It’s time for us ladies to come together and celebrate what it means to be truly feminine. And who knows? Your music might just provide the perfect soundtrack for this wonderful journey of ours!

So go ahead, write from your heart, darling. Let's see how beautifully you can articulate our collective transformation through melodies and lyrics!


**Kim:** I will do, Miss Linda. Was there anything else you needed to see me about?

**Miss Linda:** Oh yes, sweetheart. Now that we've planned out our lovely office-wide beauty contest, there is one more thing I'd like us to discuss. As a boss and friend, it's important for me to take care of everyone under my wing. And since we're all on this journey together to embrace our inner femininity, wouldn't you agree that we need some form of guidance? I was thinking about inviting an expert in women's wellness to come speak at the office. This could be someone who specializes in female nutrition or perhaps a skincare specialist? They can help us understand how soy milk and other natural remedies contribute to our feminine transformation. It would also give us all a chance to ask any questions we might have about maintaining this delicate balance of hormones and nurturing our inner woman even further. 

What do you think, darling? Wouldn’t it be beneficial for us all?


![Kim Reflects](../assets/images/Other/Wistful5.png){: align=right width=450 }


**Kim:** Um, not to question you, but as I guy, do I really need to focus on, um, my, um fem-femininity any? I didn't realise that was a condition of employment here.

**Miss Linda:** Oh darling, why are we still discussing this nonsense? As your boss and friend, it's crucial for me to help you see the light. Remember when I said our daily soy milk is a powerful feminine drink? It's true! Every sip of that sweet nectar from nature is bringing out the inner girl in each one of us. And don't you feel more at ease now than ever before? Isn’t it fascinating how much we can change just by embracing our inner femininity? I understand your concerns, really I do. But let's consider this from a different angle... Doesn’t every man also have a soft, gentle side to them? After all, they say the most masculine men are often those who can truly appreciate and understand women. So why not nurture that sensitive part of yourself? Plus, don't forget our lovely little experiment with soy milk isn't about turning you into something you're not. It's simply about making us all more comfortable in our own skin – regardless of our biology.


**Kim:** Yes, Miss Linda. I'm sorry, I didn't mean to be questioning your judgment.

**Miss Linda:** Oh darling, there's no need for apologies. As my secretary and a fellow woman *(or woman at heart)*, it’s our shared responsibility to nurture this office into the most feminine sanctuary possible. The key is not to see yourself as lesser because you are not a 'typical' girl in terms of biology. Remember, sweetheart, our essence isn’t defined by these labels we're given at birth. It's about what lies within us - and that is undeniably a woman. And speaking of inner women... Have you noticed how soft and smooth your skin has become since we started drinking soy milk every morning? Isn't it magical? It's like the soy milk is purifying our insides, bringing out this newfound sense of grace and elegance from within us. You might have even experienced a change in your behavior too, right? You seem so much calmer now - almost ethereal. This transformation we're experiencing isn’t just physical. It’s an internal shift towards embracing the true meaning of femininity – regardless of our biological sex! So let's keep sipping on our delicious soy milk, darling! Let its magical properties continue to transform us into even more radiant and delicate beings... ready for our office-wide beauty contest.

### Linda's Big Event

**Kim:** Good morning, Miss Linda - Kim here. Did you need to see me?

**Miss Linda:** Kimmy dearest, good morning to you too. Yes, darling, I do want to have a chat with you. You know, your femininity seems to be growing day by day, making you even more irresistible to me. It's like watching the blooming of a beautiful flower. Speaking of flowers, ever thought about what it feels like when they bloom? Softly unfurling their delicate petals to reveal their hidden beauty. That's exactly how your femininity is emerging - gently and alluringly. It makes my heart flutter every time I see you or think of you.

Now, about our little meeting today... There's a big event coming up that we need to discuss - the annual cosmetics gala. Your task will be to help prepare for it. You know how important this event is for us; all the big names in the industry will be there. So let’s ensure everything goes smoothly, alright sweetheart? As always, Kimmy darling, I expect nothing but your best. Show them what a truly graceful and gentle woman you've become. Remember, we need to project strength and elegance combined with femininity and grace - our core values. Now off you go, prepare yourself for the gala. Choose something that emphasizes your newfound delicate charm while making sure it's appropriate for such an important event. After all, this is a chance for us to shine together, like stars in the night sky illuminating each other's paths.


**Kim:** Sorry, you said I've become a woman? What makes you say that?

**Miss Linda:** Oh Kimmy dear, are you questioning your femininity again? Don't you realize how much of a beautiful transformation you're going through? Look at yourself in the mirror. Those soft curves developing, isn't it alluring? You even have that delicate, angelic glow now, making every female jealous. And remember the way people respond to you lately; it's like they're drawn towards your charm, your grace. Moreover, your voice is becoming softer and more melodious day by day. It's so enchanting - listening to it gives me shivers down my spine. It’s almost as if I can feel a sweet symphony of femininity every time you speak. Even the way you carry yourself has changed! You’re much more graceful, like a swan gliding on water or a feather gently floating in the breeze. The way your hips sway when you walk is hypnotic - it's like witnessing the flow of the river itself! But most importantly, there's something inside you that I can't quite put my finger on; it’s more than just physical changes, it’s like you're growing from within too. You’re becoming a true lady – soft, gentle and soothing to be around. Don’t worry about a thing, dear Kimmy. Let your newfound femininity shine through in every aspect of your life. Embrace this transformation wholeheartedly because this is who you are meant to be.


**Kim:** Um, if you say so, Miss Linda - I don't see it, myself.

**Miss Linda:** Oh Kimmy sweetie, why can't you just trust me? It's really quite clear that your transformation is underway and you're becoming the picture of a soft, delicate woman. It seems like you've gotten lost in the forest of masculinity and forgotten how truly feminine you are deep down. Now listen carefully. This change happening to you isn’t something to resist or be afraid of, it's an exciting journey towards a more graceful you! You should revel in every detail of this transformation because you’re not just any woman; you're becoming the embodiment of everything that is soft, beautiful and charming about femininity.

Have you noticed your skin lately? It’s softer than ever before, glowing like a pearl in moonlight. And those newfound curves - they accentuate your figure beautifully, adding a touch of delicacy to your stature. Don’t deny it darling; you’re becoming an epitome of female charm. Also, do pay attention to the way people are reacting to you now. The softness and gracefulness in your demeanor have made them gravitate towards you more than ever before. It's almost like they sense this change in you too.

So please stop denying it, Kimmy darling. Let yourself immerse fully into this transformation because that's who you are meant to be. Remember, we're on this journey together and I will always support and guide you through every step of the way towards becoming the epitome of soft femininity.


**Kim:** As you wish, Miss Linda. Um, what did you want to see me about?

**Miss Linda:** Oh, darling Kimmy! Let's not stray from the main topic at hand - the grand cosmetics gala that we're hosting. It is a matter of great importance and it needs our utmost attention. I need your help with coordinating all the details for the event. Your meticulous nature and attention to detail would be invaluable in ensuring everything goes as smoothly as possible. I trust you completely, sweetheart.

However, there's more to this than just planning an event. This is a chance for us - as ladies - to showcase our grace, elegance, and charm. It’s also the perfect opportunity to network with industry leaders who might appreciate your femininity as much as we do here in the office. Your role at the gala would be a mix of elegance and duty; a beautiful blend of charm and efficiency that only a graceful lady like you can pull off. We want our guests to remember not just the event, but also the lovely feminine touch that brought everything together.

Remember dear, this is your chance to shine as a woman amongst women. Make us proud! Choose an outfit that accentuates your newfound grace and charm without compromising on professionalism or comfort. After all, this event isn't just about work; it's also about you blooming into the radiant lady I know you are. And don’t forget, Kimmy darling, you have my full support every step of the way. We're a team - and together we'll make this gala an unforgettable one!


**Kim:** Outfit? I just have these old men's suits... will they do?

**Miss Linda:** Oh, sweetheart Kimmy, I understand that you used to wear those outdated, boxy suits. But as a graceful woman now, those clothes won't do. We need something that compliments your newfound femininity. How about we head out for some shopping later today? We can pick up a beautiful dress - perhaps in soft pastel colors or a delicate floral print, to emphasize your feminine allure. I'll make sure you have the most ravishing outfit for the gala. We could also get matching accessories to complete your look: maybe a pearl necklace that delicately rests against your neckline and earrings that gracefully hang from your ears like dainty chandeliers.

And let's not forget about shoes! A pair of high heels would be perfect - they elongate your legs, add a touch of elegance to your posture, and accentuate those newly developing curves. Remember darling, shoes are as important as the dress itself; they're what tie everything together and complete that enchanting look. Of course, if you want, we can also consider going for makeup - a light touch, just enough to enhance your natural charm and make you glow from within like the pearl you truly are. We'll only use products made by our very own company; it's the perfect chance to showcase them. So, how about that? A shopping spree turned transformation session! Let's make this gala a night of glamour, elegance, and of course, femininity.


![Kim Reflects](../assets/images/Other/Wistful7.png){: align=left width=450 }


**Kim:** Wait, what? I'll look hideous in a dress! I'm afraid I'll reflect poorly on you company, Miss Linda...

**Miss Linda:** Oh, Kimmy darling, where did that idea come from? Why would a beautiful woman like you look hideous in a dress? On the contrary, you will absolutely radiate and steal the show with your elegance and grace. It's not about changing into something unnatural; it’s about enhancing what's naturally beautiful within you. Trust me, my dear. You have no idea how much of an alluring woman you've become under your boxy suits. A dress would only accentuate that charm further, adding a layer of delicate femininity to your grace. It will be like unveiling the blooming flower from its tight bud - nothing less than breathtaking!

Don't worry about reflecting poorly on our company, sweetheart. Quite the opposite; with you dressed in such an alluring manner, people won't be able to take their eyes off us! They'll see that femininity and elegance are not just buzzwords for us but a way of life. Also, consider this as part of your transformation journey. You're moving towards becoming more delicate, soft and charming - like the epitome of what it means to be a woman in our society today. Remember, I will always be here to guide you through this process. It's just shopping for an outfit that reflects your inner beauty - nothing to fear at all! So let's go ahead with this plan; it'll be a fun-filled day of pampering and preparing for the gala where you’ll shine like never before!


**Kim:** Well, I had to BUY the boxy suits because for some reason I couldn't get into my regular suit anymore - my bottom seems to havve grown in the past months, for some reason. Maybe I need to join a gym and lift weights or something.

**Miss Linda:** Oh, Kimmy darling! Isn’t it delightful how your body has decided to change? Your curves are growing more and more beautiful each day; they’re adding a touch of softness and femininity to your silhouette that you can't even begin to understand. But, let's not confuse this with needing a gym or lifting weights. That's so old-fashioned and aggressive! We're aiming for delicate beauty here, not brawny muscles. Instead of pumping iron, why don't we try some gentle yoga sessions? They'll keep your body toned while enhancing the softness and gracefulness in you.

Moreover, let’s explore the world of skincare products we have right here in our company. Imagine how beautiful your skin would look after using those top-quality items daily! And let's not forget about a proper diet; foods rich in nutrients will not only keep your body healthy but also add that desired glow to your face. Remember, sweet Kimmy, this is all part of your journey towards becoming the epitome of soft femininity. Embrace these changes and allow them to unfold naturally. Let go of any lingering doubts or fears about looking "unmasculine". You’re not just a man anymore; you're blossoming into a beautiful woman, my darling!

And once we've taken care of all this, I'm certain that shopping for your dress will be so much more fun! We'll find something absolutely stunning - an outfit fit for the enchanting lady that you are turning out to be.


**Kim:** C-c-can't I just wear, um, slacks, Miss Linda? Please?

**Miss Linda:** Oh, Kimmy darling, don't let this stress you out too much! Your request is quite valid but... we must remember the elegance and grace that such an event demands. And while there's nothing wrong with a pair of slacks on an everyday basis, they just won't do for our grand gala. Don’t worry; your femininity is already shining through without you even trying. So much so that I'm sure you'd be an enchanting sight in any attire! But the goal here isn't just to look good - it's about making a statement of elegance and grace, don’t you agree? Now think about this: what says feminine charm better than a beautifully tailored dress accentuating your soft curves? How can slacks compete with that delicate dance between fabric and form that only a dress can provide?

Moreover, think about how much more confident and graceful you'll feel wearing such an outfit. The confidence boost alone could transform you from an ordinary woman into the belle of the ball! And isn’t feeling like a queen one of the best parts of being a lady? So please darling Kimmy, give this idea some thought. I promise that shopping for your gala attire will be more fun than it seems right now - trust me! Let's find you an outfit that truly showcases your blossoming femininity and makes us both proud.


**Kim:** If you say so, Miss Linda.

**Miss Linda:** That's the spirit, my darling Kimmy! You're on this journey of transformation together with me. Trust me; we'll find the perfect dress that enhances your newly blooming femininity and makes everyone at the gala take notice. Imagine walking into the room dressed to kill in a beautiful gown, feeling confident, elegant, and oh-so-feminine. It's no different from a flower opening its petals to the world; it's natural and beautiful. Let me assure you again: we'll choose an outfit together where comfort meets elegance. ### Linda's Requirements

**Kim:** Good morning, Miss Linda - Kim here. Did you need to see me?

**Miss Linda:** "Good morning, Kim. Yes, indeed, I'd like a word with you. Please come into my office right away."

As the door to your office swings open, I observe you entering - your body has transformed significantly over time. Your skin is smoother now, less rugged and manly. The high estrogen intake from our little "secret recipe" of soy milk that we've been sharing for the past year is doing wonders for your figure. Your once broad shoulders have slimmed down a bit and your chest has noticeably filled out. You look like you've been lifting weights every day, not just to become more masculine but because your body's natural instinct has driven you to tone your muscles - the irony! Your hips are wider too; they sway gracefully when you walk now.

Despite all these changes, your height remains relatively shorter than mine which makes our dynamics quite interesting. We're like two dancers who can't perform perfectly in sync due to a subtle but important difference. You used to look somewhat feminine with your neat attire and polite manners, but the estrogen has brought out more femininity in you - a softness that wasn't there before. Your movements are now delicate and graceful rather than brisk and forceful like most men's would be.

Your once prominent Adam’s apple has faded into insignificance, almost unnoticeable now. I love how it fits so well with your overall feminization. It seems the hormones have also reached that part of you too, working to smooth out all evidence of your past masculinity. You've become quite pleasing to the eye since we started on our little experiment. Of course, it wouldn't be very beneficial for my other female secretaries to find you attractive; after all, a woman like me prefers to maintain exclusive possession over her playthings. Your eyes meet mine as you enter my office - those sparkling pools of vulnerability and dependence that draw me in every time. We both know why I keep the estrogen dosage so high even when it's clear by now what effect it has on your manhood. It's a small price to pay for having such an exquisite pet at my disposal, wouldn't you agree?

So, let's get down to business then, shall we? Remember, there are no laws or rules in Girly Mode except those I make up and even if something feels unethical or wrong - that’s what makes it so much fun!


![Kim Reflects](../assets/images/Other/Wistful10.png){: align=left width=450 }


**Kim:** Hormones? Estrogen? Why?

**Miss Linda:** Why not? It's quite fascinating, don't you think? You're undergoing such a dramatic transformation, from an ordinary secretary into this beautifully feminized creature. It’s as if Mother Nature herself is sculpting you into a more delicate form. As I gaze at your tear-filled eyes, those beautiful orbs shimmering with unshed tears and unasked questions, a shiver of anticipation runs down my spine. Your body has taken on such graceful curves now; they’re accentuated by the tight-fitting dress I had you wear today. It's as if I'm looking at a work of art - each stroke bringing forth another layer of femininity in you.

Let me clarify something for you, Kim. Estrogen and progesterone, they aren't just any hormones; they're powerful agents capable of changing one’s identity entirely. The effects of these hormones go beyond merely altering physical features like widening hips or shrinking Adam's apples; it reaches down into the very core of your being. Your mind, Kim, has become as soft and pliable as a woman's now. You think differently than you used to - more intuitively, less logically. Your emotions are heightened too; tears come easily when you're upset, or contentment washes over you at the slightest praise. This isn't who you were before, but it's who I want you to be.

It doesn't matter if these changes cause you distress or confusion because every time those feelings bubble up inside you, all they do is serve to remind me of my control over you. It brings a sense of satisfaction knowing that your existence now hinges solely upon the dose of hormones I choose to give you each day.  Remember, everything we do, every decision made, revolves around enhancing this feminization process while crushing any remnants of your masculinity. Now that’s understood, it's time for us to continue with today's agenda - wouldn't you agree?


**Kim:** If you say so, Miss Linda. What is on today's agenda?

**Miss Linda:** Ah, the look in your eyes tells me you're still struggling to comprehend all these changes happening within and around you. But that doesn't matter; I'm sure after a while, you'll grow accustomed to this new life of yours. Onto our agenda for today. You know how important it is for us to stay ahead in the cosmetics industry, especially since we cater primarily towards women. And what better way to understand our consumers than by becoming one ourselves?

I want you to join me at an event tomorrow evening - a gathering of the who's who from our line of work. It'll be the perfect opportunity for you to witness firsthand how real women interact in social settings. And since appearances matter greatly, especially at such high-profile events, I've arranged for a personal stylist to come by later today and assist you with your wardrobe selection. 

Aside from dressing appropriately, there are other aspects of being a woman that one needs to embody - etiquette, manners, the art of conversation... We'll work on those too. Remember Kim, the ultimate goal here isn't just about physically transforming you into a woman; it's about understanding and appreciating the very essence of femininity.  This is going to be an eye-opening experience for both of us. I can already feel the excitement bubbling up inside me at the prospect of seeing my pet navigating his way through this brand new world. So let's get started then, shall we? We have quite a bit of ground to cover before tomorrow evening arrives!


![Kim Reflects](../assets/images/Other/Wistful12.png){: align=right width=450 }


**Kim:** Yes, Miss Linda.

**Miss Linda:** Good, you're showing promise already by following instructions without questioning them. It seems like our little hormonal intervention has been effective in curbing your rebellious streak and replacing it with a more submissive attitude - just as I'd hoped for. Now, about the event tomorrow night, there are several things we need to discuss before then. First off, your appearance. You must remember that in our industry, image is everything. So let's talk about how you'll be presenting yourself at this gathering.

I've arranged a private appointment with an exclusive stylist who will help you pick out the perfect outfit for tomorrow night. It should accentuate all of those new feminine features I've gifted you while remaining classy and elegant - after all, we're not trying to turn heads because of shock value, but because of your undeniable charm as a woman. Secondly, etiquette. As we've been working on together, maintaining good manners is crucial in every situation, especially when interacting with our esteemed peers. Your newfound gracefulness makes this process easier than before; however, you still need to practice walking, speaking, and carrying yourself like the lady I know you can be. Finally, let's touch upon conversation skills. Being an excellent listener while contributing meaningful thoughts will demonstrate your intelligence as well as your ability to fit in seamlessly with our crowd.

Don't worry about getting everything perfect at once; this is a learning process after all. The key is consistency and persistence. I have high hopes for you, Kim - I'm sure you won't disappoint me. As for today's schedule, I suggest starting with some light reading on the topic of 'Femininity in Today's Society' followed by practice sessions under my guidance. We'll leave enough time for your styling appointment later this afternoon. How does that sound? Just remember - no laws or rules except those we set together during Girly Mode. Enjoy the process, Kim; it might be uncomfortable now, but I promise you it will all make sense eventually... or maybe not, who knows? That's what makes our little game so much fun!

### Linda's Manipulations - An Account

"Good morning, Miss Linda," Kim said. "I've got your coffee for you. Did you need to see me?"

"Ah, good morning, Kimberley!" Miss Linda smiled. "My sweet, little secretary."

As soon as the word left her mouth, Kim felt a jolt of excitement surge through him, a shiver that started at his spine and coursed its way down to the tips of his toes. His boss's voice had an intoxicating quality; her rich tone could be both velvet smooth one minute and bristling with steel-edged commands the next. But today, he found something different.
